## Notes

- Trades are sorted by date (newest first), then by NFT edition number
- XCH Equivalent is calculated using TibetSwap/Dexie exchange rates for CAT tokens
- USD values are calculated using the current XCH/USD rate of $4.2/XCH
  - **Note:** Historical XCH/USD rates vary significantly. For accurate USD values, fetch historical rates from CoinGecko API for each trade date
- Attribute prices are calculated by dividing the total NFT price by 7 (number of attributes)
- This data is sourced from Dexie.space API (completed trades only, status=4)
- Collection: Wojak Farmers Plot (4,200 NFTs on Chia blockchain)
- If an NFT was sold multiple times, only the most recent sale is shown in the "Unique NFTs Sold Summary"
